                                            {{#if translation}} {{! 翻訳あり }}
                                                <a href="/search.php?s_mode=s_tag_full&word={{url_encode tag}}"
                                                    class="text js-click-trackable-later"
                                                    data-click-category="illust-tag-on-member-illust-medium"

                                                    data-click-label="translation-tag"
                                                >
                                                    {{tag}}
                                                    <span class="illust-tag-translation">{{translation}}</span>
                                                </a>
                                            {{else if romaji}} {{! ローマ字あり }}
                                                <a href="/search.php?s_mode=s_tag_full&word={{url_encode tag}}"
                                                    class="text js-click-trackable-later"
                                                    data-click-category="illust-tag-on-member-illust-medium"

                                                    data-click-label="romaji-tag"
                                                >

                                                </a>
                                            {{else}} {{! 翻訳もローマ字もない場合 }}
                                                <a href="/search.php?s_mode=s_tag_full&word={{url_encode tag}}"
                                                    class="text js-click-trackable-later"
                                                    data-click-category="illust-tag-on-member-illust-medium"

                                                    data-click-label="original-tag"
                                                >
                                                    {{tag}}
                                                </a>
                                            {{/if}}
                                            <a href="https://dic.pixiv.net/a/{{url_encode tag}}" target="_blank" class="icon-pixpedia{{#unless is_pixpedia_article_exists}}-no-item{{/unless}} _ui-tooltip" data-tooltip="{{#if is_pixpedia_article_exists}}Articles about 「{{tag}}」 {{else}}Create an article related to {{tag}}{{/if}}"></a>
                                        </li>
                                    {{/tags}}
                                </ul>
                            {{else}}
                                <span class="no-item">No tags were used.</span>
                            {{/if}}
                        </script>
